A scheme is the\n38: // foundation for a versioned API and versioned configuration over time.\n39: //\n40: // In a Scheme, a Type is a particular Go struct, a Version is a point-in-time\n41: // identifier for a particular representation of that Type (typically backwards\n42: // compatible), a Kind is the unique name for that Type within the Version, and a\n43: // Group identifies a set of Versions, Kinds, and Types that evolve over time. An\n44: // Unversioned Type is one that is not yet formally bound to a type and is promised\n45: // to be backwards compatible (effectively a \"v1\" of a Type that does not expect\n46: // to break in Code Generation for DeepCopyObject\\nThe deepcopy-gen code generator (controlled by the `// +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object` directive in type definitions) automatically generates `DeepCopyObject()` methods for all core/v1 types. These implementations are in `zz_generated.deepcopy.go` and delegate to the generated `DeepCopy()` method.\\n\\nCore/v1 types implementing runtime.Object include:\\n- **Pod** - Container execution unit\\n- **Node** - Cluster node resource\\n- **Service** - Network service abstraction\\n- **Namespace** - Resource grouping and isolation\\n- **Binding** - Pod-to-node binding\\n- **Event** - API event record\\n- **PersistentVolume** & **PersistentVolumeClaim** - Storage abstractions\\n- **Secret** & **ConfigMap** - Configuration storage\\n- **ServiceAccount** - Authentication identity\\n- **ReplicationController** - Workload replication (legacy)\\n- **PodTemplate** - Pod template definition\\n- **Endpoints** - Service endpoint address list\\n- **LimitRange** & **ResourceQuota** - Resource constraints\\n- **ComponentStatus** - Component health status\\n- **RangeAllocation** & **SerializedReference** - Internal types\\n- **Pod*Options** types (AttachOptions, LogOptions, ExecOptions, PortForwardOptions, ProxyOptions)\\n- **ServiceProxyOptions** & **NodeProxyOptions** - Proxy configuration\\n- Plus corresponding List types for all resources\\n\\n### 4. Scheme Registration Pattern\\nThe Kubernetes Scheme provides the type registry for runtime.Object implementations. The scheme is built using:\\n\\n1. **SchemeBuilder** (`pkg/runtime/scheme_builder.go`) - A builder pattern that collects registration functions\\n2. **Scheme** (`pkg/runtime/scheme.go`) - Manages mappings between Go types and Kubernetes GroupVersionKind metadata\\n3. **addKnownTypes function** (`staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/register.go`) - Explicitly registers all core/v1 types with their GroupVersion\\n\\nThe registration in core/v1/register.go creates a SchemeBuilder with `runtime.NewSchemeBuilder(addKnownTypes)` and exposes it via `AddToScheme`, enabling each package to declaratively register its API types with any Scheme.\\n\\n### 5. Type and Meta Implementation\\nThe `TypeMeta` and `ObjectMeta` types from `k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/meta.go` provide the base fields that enable runtime.Object implementation. These implementations are in `zz_generated.deepcopy.go` and delegate to the generated `DeepCopy()` method.\\n\\nCore/v1 types implementing runtime.Object include:\\n- **Pod** - Container execution unit\\n- **Node** - Cluster node resource\\n- **Service** - Network service abstraction\\n- **Namespace** - Resource grouping and isolation\\n- **Binding** - Pod-to-node binding\\n- **Event** - API event record\\n- **PersistentVolume** & **PersistentVolumeClaim** - Storage abstractions\\n- **Secret** & **ConfigMap** - Configuration storage\\n- **ServiceAccount** - Authentication identity\\n- **ReplicationController** - Workload replication (legacy)\\n- **PodTemplate** - Pod template definition\\n- **Endpoints** - Service endpoint address list\\n- **LimitRange** & **ResourceQuota** - Resource constraints\\n- **ComponentStatus** - Component health status\\n- **RangeAllocation** & **SerializedReference** - Internal types\\n- **Pod*Options** types (AttachOptions, LogOptions, ExecOptions, PortForwardOptions, ProxyOptions)\\n- **ServiceProxyOptions** & **NodeProxyOptions** - Proxy configuration\\n- Plus corresponding List types for all resources\\n\\n### 4. Scheme Registration Pattern\\nThe Kubernetes Scheme provides the type registry for runtime.Object implementations. The scheme is built using:\\n\\n1. **SchemeBuilder** (`pkg/runtime/scheme_builder.go`) - A builder pattern that collects registration functions\\n2. **Scheme** (`pkg/runtime/scheme.go`) - Manages mappings between Go types and Kubernetes GroupVersionKind metadata\\n3. **addKnownTypes function** (`staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/register.go`) - Explicitly registers all core/v1 types with their GroupVersion\\n\\nThe registration in core/v1/register.go creates a SchemeBuilder with `runtime.NewSchemeBuilder(addKnownTypes)` and exposes it via `AddToScheme`, enabling each package to declaratively register its API types with any Scheme.\\n\\n### 5. scheme\\n\\nThis design decouples API type definitions from the runtime machinery, allowing the same Object interface and Scheme infrastructure to work across all Kubernetes API groups and
